    <script>
        function showTrending() {
            var nbDeviceWidth = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientWidth || 0, window.innerWidth || 0);
            var nbScrollWidth = document.querySelector("#nav__trending_topics .modul--trending").scrollWidth;
            var trendingWrapper = document.querySelector('.nb_trending_wrapper');
            if (nbScrollWidth > nbDeviceWidth) {
                trendingWrapper.classList.remove('dis0');
            }
        }

        showTrending();
    </script>

                            <script type="application/javascript">
                    observeTeaserSlider('.tm-75557087')
                    function observeTeaserSlider(teaserModuleId) {
                        const teaserStage = document.querySelector('.teaser-slider-stage' + teaserModuleId);
                        if (!teaserStage) return;
                        const teaserStageObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
                            if (entries[0].isIntersecting) {
                                setTimeout(function () {
                                    sliderTeaser(teaserModuleId);
                                }, 500);
                                teaserStageObserver.disconnect();
                            }
                        });
                        teaserStageObserver.observe(teaserStage);
                    }
                </script>
